<div class="section" id="sec5"><div class="header article-hdr"><div class="kicker">		                        SECTION V.</div><h2>Implementation of DLL-Based SSCG</h2></div><p><a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig11" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 11</a> shows a block diagram of the proposed DLL-based SSCG. The proposed SSCG can be separated into three blocks; i.e., delay cell array (DCA), DLL, and modulator profile generator (MPG). While the DCA generates a total of 256 phases by using 128 differential delay cells, the DLL accurately aligns the phase from <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-64-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-943" role="math" style="width: 1.444em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.26em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-944"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-945"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-946" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-947"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-948"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-949" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-64">D_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-65-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-950" role="math" style="width: 2.225em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.99em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-951"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-952"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-953" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-954"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-955"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-956" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">256</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-65">D_{256}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. After the calibration in the DLL is completed, the MPG begins to generate an 8-bit modulation code <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-66-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-957" role="math" style="width: 3.607em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.246em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1003.13em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-958"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-959" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-960"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-961" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">P<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.123em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-962"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-963"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-964" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-965" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-966" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-967" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-66">(P_{\rm MOD})</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. In order to achieve better EMI reduction, the MPG generates an H-K modulation profile by utilizing the slope-modulation technique <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref5" id="context_ref_5_5">[5]</a>. An 8-bit MUX in the DCA then finally synthesizes the output spread-spectrum clock <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-67-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-968" role="math" style="width: 2.946em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.646em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.53em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-969"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-970" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-971"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.865em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-972" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-973"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-974"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-975" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">S</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-976" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">S</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-977" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-978" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-67">(f_{\rm SSC})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> by shuffling the phases in accordance with <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-68-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-979" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.47em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-980"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-981"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-982" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">P<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.123em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-983"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-984"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-985" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-986" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-987" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-68">P_{\rm MOD}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>.
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig11"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-11-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-11-small.gif" alt="Figure 11" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 11. </b><fig><p>Block diagram of the proposed DLL-based SSCG.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7051289/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
<div class="figure figure-full" id="fig12"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-12-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-12-small.gif" alt="Figure 12" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 12. </b><fig><p>(a) Block diagram of DCA, (b) UDC, and (c) load cell.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7051289/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
<p></p><div class="section_2" id="sec5a"><h3>A. DCA</h3><p><a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig12" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 12</a> describes the block diagram of the DCA, its unit delay cell (UDC), and the load cell. As seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig12" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 12(a)</a>, the DCA is composed of 16×8 UDCs and 16 load cells along with logic decoders. In the DCA, the UDCs are arranged in a zigzag manner to minimize an abrupt delay change between delay cells in a row-switching operation. The 8-bit phase-modulation code, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-69-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-988" role="math" style="width: 5.709em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 5.108em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1004.99em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-989"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-990"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-991" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">P<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-72">P_{\rm MOD} \langle 3:0\rangle</script></tex-math></inline-formula>) and utilized to drive the differential switch in the load cell, 3-bit row decoder, and 4-bit column decoder, respectively. As shown in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig12" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 12(b)</a>, the UDC is designed with two nMOS transistors driven with a differential signal from the previous cell where the load consists of a pair of cross-coupled pMOS along with another pair of current driven pMOS whose current is adjusted by <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-73-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1042" role="math" style="width: 2.946em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.646em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.65em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1043"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1044"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.646em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1045" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">V<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.183em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1046"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1047"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1048" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1049" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">T</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1050" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">R</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1051" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-73">V_{\rm CTRL}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The outputs of each UDC are connected to a subsequent nMOS transistor that is accompanied by a cascode switch for the row selection of the DCA. Thus, each UDC drives the same load despite the change in the MUX. As can be seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig12" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 12(c)</a>, the same configuration of the load as that of the DCA is connected to the nodes, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-74-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1052" role="math" style="width: 0.844em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.724em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1000.72em 2.345em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1053"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1054" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">Z<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-74">Z</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-75-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1055" role="math" style="width: 0.904em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.784em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.964em 1000.78em 2.345em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1056"><span class="munderover" id="MathJax-Span-1057"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.784em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.72em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1058" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">Z<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.306em 1000.72em 3.847em -999.997em); left: -0.057em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">¯</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.021em; left: 0.423em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">¯</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.021em; left: 0.123em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">¯</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.021em; left: 0.303em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">¯</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-75">\overline{Z}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, for the column selection. The DCA consumes 23.5 mW of average power from a 1.8-V supply.</p></div><div class="section_2" id="sec5b"><h3>B. DLL</h3><p>
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig13"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-13-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-13-small.gif" alt="Figure 13" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 13. </b><fig><p>Schematic of DCCS.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7051289/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
The DLL in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig11" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 11</a> is composed of a bang–bang phase detector (BBPD), an 8-bit up/down counter, a lock detector, and a digitally controlled current source (DCCS). Similar to the conventional digital DLL, the BBPD compares <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-76-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1060" role="math" style="width: 1.444em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.26em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1061"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1062"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1063" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1064"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1065"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1066" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-76">D_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-77-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1067" role="math" style="width: 2.225em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.99em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1068"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1069"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1070" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1071"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1072"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1073" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">256</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-77">D_{256}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and then delivers an up/down order sign to the subsequent 8-bit counter. The up/down counter generates an 8-bit calibration code to the DCCS and eventually produces the control voltage, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-78-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1074" role="math" style="width: 2.946em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.646em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.65em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1075"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1076"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.646em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1077" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">V<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.183em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1078"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1079"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1080" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1081" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">T</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1082" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">R</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1083" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-78">V_{\rm CTRL}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig13" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 13</a> describes the schematic of the DCCS. As seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig13" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 13</a>, the DCCS consists of switch-controlled nMOS cascade current sources with a pMOS diode load. It is noted that the 4-bit least significant bit (LSB) is converted into a thermometer code to improve the monotonicity by driving the identical current cell while the 4-bit MSB sustains its intrinsic binary format. The DCCS-controlled current is set as <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-79-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1084" role="math" style="width: 16.64em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 14.958em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1014.84em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1085"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1086"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.405em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.3em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1087" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">i</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.363em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1088"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1089"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1090" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1091" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1092" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1093" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">S</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1094" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;"> </span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1095" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">[</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1096" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1097"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1098"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1099"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1100"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1101" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">A</span></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1102" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">]</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1103" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1104" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">10</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1105" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.243em;">+</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1106" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.243em;">0.5</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1107" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.243em;">⋅</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1108" style="padding-left: 0.243em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1109"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1110" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1111" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">A</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1112" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1113" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">⟨</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1114" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">7</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1115" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">:</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1116" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1117" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">⟩</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-79">i_{\rm DCCS}~[\mu{\hbox{A}}] = 10 + 0.5 \cdot {\rm CAL}\langle 7:0\rangle</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, where <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-80-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1118" role="math" style="width: 5.288em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 4.748em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1004.63em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1119"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1120"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1121"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1122" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1123" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">A</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1124" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1125" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">⟨</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1126" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">7</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1127" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">:</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1128" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1129" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">⟩</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-80">{\rm CAL}\langle7:0\rangle</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is an 8-bit code of the up/down counter. Moreover, a lock detector is used to eliminate the voltage-sensitive jitter by preserving the value after delay calibration. Once the difference between <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-81-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1130" role="math" style="width: 1.444em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.26em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1131"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1132"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1133" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1134"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1135"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1136" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-81">D_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-82-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1137" role="math" style="width: 2.225em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.99em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1138"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1139"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1140" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1141"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1142"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1143" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">256</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-82">D_{256}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is small enough not to differentiate, the BBPD produces a lock signal and then the subsequent lock detector generates a hold flag to cut the calibration loop in the case where four lock signals are generated in series. The DLL consumes 210 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-83-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1144" role="math" style="width: 1.805em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.625em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1001.63em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1145"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1146" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1147"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1148"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1149"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1150"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1151" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">W</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-83">\mu{\hbox{W}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> from 1.8-V supply.<p></p></div><div class="section_2" id="sec5c"><h3>C. Modulation Profile Generator</h3><p>
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig14"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-14-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/22/7078974/7051289/7051289-fig-14-small.gif" alt="Figure 14" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 14. </b><fig><p>(a) Block diagram of MPG, (b) timing diagram of MPG, and (c) effect of H-k profile.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/7051289/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
As shown in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig14" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 14(a)</a>, the MPG consists of a triangular generator, a 20-bit accumulator, a DSM, and a 8-bit accumulator. The MPG in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig11" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 11</a> starts to generate the modulation code in accordance with the enable signal from the lock detector after the delay calibration is completed. In order to alleviate the edge concentrated spectrum power in a triangular profile, a nonlinear modulation profile called an H-K <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref9" id="context_ref_9_5c">[9]</a> is utilized. The H-K modulation profile is well known as an optimal modulation profile for spread-spectrum clock generation when the modulation frequency is below the resolution bandwidth (RBW) of the spectrum analyzer <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref10" id="context_ref_10_5c">[10]</a>. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig14" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 14(b)</a> shows the corresponding timing diagram of each constituting block in the MPG for H-K profile generation. As can be seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig14" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 14(b)</a>, the triangular generator first produces a slope profile with a double modulation frequency <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-84-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1152" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.38em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1153"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1154" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1155"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1156" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1157"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1158"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1159" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-84">2f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> that is constrained to the starting point, offset, and the unit incremental size, step. A subsequent 20-bit accumulator then generates the H-K profile by integrating the output of the slope generator with a modulation frequency of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-85-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1160" role="math" style="width: 1.024em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1000.9em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1161"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1162"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1163" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1164"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1165"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1166" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-85">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The two design constraints in the slope generator (offset and step) are utilized to adjust the instantaneous slope of the H-K modulation profile, which affects the edge-concentrated spectrum power. As shown in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig14" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 14(c)</a>, the edge-concentrated power is more reduced while the instantaneous slope of the H-K profile changes more radically. Following the 20-bit accumulator, the DSM is utilized to quantize the 20-bit H-K modulation profile into a 4-bit length frequency profile. Thereafter, an 8-bit accumulator, whose number of bits corresponds to the number of phases in the DCA, converts the frequency profile <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-86-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1167" role="math" style="width: 3.426em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.066em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.95em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1168"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1169" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1170"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.285em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1171" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1172"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1173"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1174" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1175" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1176" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1177" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-86">(f_{\rm MOD})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> to a direct phase profile <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-87-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1178" role="math" style="width: 3.607em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.246em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1003.13em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1179"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1180" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1181"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1182" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">P<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.123em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1183"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1184"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1185" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1186" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1187" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1188" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-87">(P_{\rm MOD})</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. This <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-88-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1189" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.47em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1190"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1191"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1192" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">P<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.123em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1193"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1194"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1195" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">M</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1196" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">O</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1197" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">D</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-89">f_{\rm SSC}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, is achieved.

<div class="section" id="sec6"><div class="header article-hdr"><div class="kicker">		                        SECTION VI.</div><h2>Experimental Results</h2></div><p><a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig15" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 15</a> shows the measured waveform and timing diagram of the MPG, the measured peak power reduction from the H-K modulation profile, and frequency spread modes of the proposed SSCG. As seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig15" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 15(a) and (b)</a>, each block in the MPG generates the expected results, as explained in <a ref-type="sec" anchor="sec5c" class="fulltext-link">Section V-C</a>, while the phase calibration completes within 6 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-90-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1207" role="math" style="width: 1.144em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.024em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1000.96em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1208"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1209" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1210"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1211"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1212"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1213"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1214" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">s</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-90">\mu{\hbox{s}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. After calibration, <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-91-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1215" role="math" style="width: 1.745em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.565em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.57em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1216"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1217" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Δ</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1218" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">T<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.123em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-91">\Delta T</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is set to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-92-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1219" role="math" style="width: 11.174em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 10.033em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1009.97em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1220"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1221" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1222"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1223"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1224" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">/</span></span></span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1225" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">19.2</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1226" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;"> </span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1227"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1228"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1229"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1230"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1231" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">MHz</span></span></span></span></span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1232"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1233"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1234" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">/</span></span></span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1235" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">256</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1236" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1237" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">203</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-92">1/19.2\ {\hbox{MHz}}/256 = 203</script></tex-math></inline-formula> ps at 19.2-MHz operating frequency. The measured peak power reduction in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig15" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 15(c)</a> reaches more than 20 dB in 7% deviation setup at 19.2-MHz operating frequency. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig15" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 15(d)</a> proves that the proposed SSCG offers an up/center/down spread mode. As for spur rejection, we measured three cases: the reference spur rejection when all digital part turns off and spur rejection when the analog and digital parts turn on with SSCG-off and SSCG-on. The purpose for three cases of spur measurement is to identify the source of spurs up to frequency as well as distinguish the spur-rejection contributions of the proposed SC-CMFB PLL and DLL-based SSCG. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig16" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 16</a> shows the measured reference spur rejection in the PLL at 925-MHz operating frequency when only the analog part of the SoC turns on. As seen in the figure, the reference spur rejection at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-93-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1238" role="math" style="width: 1.024em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1000.9em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1239"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1240"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1241" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1242"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1243"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1244" style="font-size: 70.7%; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-93">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> (19.2 MHz) is measured down to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-94-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1245" role="math" style="width: 2.045em; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-94">{-}{\hbox{94}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> dBc, while the rejection at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-95-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1255" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.38em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1256"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1257" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1258"><span style="display: inline-block; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.805em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1001.8em 2.405em -999.997em); width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-96">{-}{\hbox{87}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> dBc at 29-dBm TX output power. This proves that the proposed DPLL suppresses the reference spurs enough to satisfy the spur specification in ARIB-T107. When all digital parts, except the SSCG, turns on in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig17" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 17(a)</a>, both spurs at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-97-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1273" role="math" style="width: 1.024em; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-97">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-98-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1280" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-98">2f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> are raised. Especially for the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-99-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1288" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.38em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1289"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1290" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1291"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1292" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1293"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1294"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1295" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-99">2f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> spur, spur rejection performance is more degraded. Finally, when all parts of the SoC including the proposed SSCG turn on, all the spurs are mitigated down to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-100-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1296" role="math" style="width: 3.426em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.066em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1003.01em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1297"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1298"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1299"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1300" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&lt;</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1301" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.243em;">−</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1302" style="padding-left: 0.243em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1303"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1304"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1305"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1306" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">80</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.13em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-100">{&lt;}-{\hbox{80}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> dBc at 25-dBm TX output power, which satisfies ARIB-T107 spur specification. As can be seen in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig17" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 17(b)</a>, it is intuitively noted that the spectrum of the spurs at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-101-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1307" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.38em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1308"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1309" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1310"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1311" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1312"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1313"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1314" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-101">2f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is spread around and its peak power reduced more than 10 dB. From these three measurements, we can recognize that the DPLL dominantly contributes the spur rejection at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-102-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1315" role="math" style="width: 1.024em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1000.9em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1316"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1317"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1318" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1319"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1320"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1321" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-102">f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, while the SSCG does at <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-103-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1322" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.38em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1323"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1324" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1325"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1326" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1327"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1328"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1329" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-103">2f_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The proposed UHF-band RFID TX is implemented in a 0.18-<inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-104-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1330" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1001.44em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1331"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1332" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1333"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1334"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1335"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1336"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1337" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-104">\mu{\hbox{m}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> CMOS process. The proposed PLL dissipates 40 mA from 2.5-V supply while all digital part including the SSCG operates at 1.8-V supply. The reason for using a higher supply in the PLL is due to the tight phase-noise specification in the ARIB-T107 specification that is not discussed in this paper. Besides, the VCO and CP use separate voltage regulators in order to avoid the spur transfer through the supply path. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig18" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 18</a> shows a micrograph of the fabricated chip. The single-chip RFID SoC including the TX, RX, modem, and processor occupies 3.8 mm×3.8 mm, while the proposed DPLL and SSCG occupy 990 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-105-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1338" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1001.44em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1339"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1340" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1341"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1342"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1343"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1344"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1345" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-105">\mu{\hbox{m}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>×900 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-106-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1346" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1001.44em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1347"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1348" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1349"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1350"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1351"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1352"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1353" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-106">\mu{\hbox{m}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and 450 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-107-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1354" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1001.44em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1355"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1356" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1357"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1358"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1359"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1360"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1361" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-107">\mu{\hbox{m}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>×450 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-108-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1362" role="math" style="width: 1.625em;
