<div class="section" id="sec7"><div class="header article-hdr"><div class="kicker">		                        SECTION VII.</div><h2>Conclusion</h2></div><p>This paper has presented a spur reduction technique for a UHF-band RFID TX using an SC-CMFB-based DPLL and a DLL-based SSCG. The proposed DPLL is characterized by adopting the SC-CMFB and distributed varactor biasing scheme to the differential CP and VCO designs, respectively. The analog parts of the SoC show down to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-109-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1370" role="math" style="width: 2.045em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.805em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1001.8em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1371"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1372"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1373"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1374" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">−</span></span></span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1375"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1376"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1377"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1378"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1379" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">94</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-109">{-}{\hbox{94}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> dBc in reference spur rejection performance at 29-dBm TX output power when all digital part turns off. Additionally, the proposed DLL-based SSCG reduces the spurious harmonic of the reference clock <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-110-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1380" role="math" style="width: 1.024em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1000.9em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1381"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1382"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.387em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1383" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.483em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1384" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-110">f_0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> due to the suppression of EMI from digital circuits. By adopting an 8-bit DLL and H-K modulated profile together, the SSCG shows more than 20-dB EMI reduction while providing the up/down/center spreading mode. Implemented in a 0.18-<inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-111-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1385" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em 1001.44em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1386"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1387" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">μ</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1388"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1389"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1390"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1391"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1392" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-111">\mu{\hbox{m}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> CMOS process, the proposed spur rejection technique allows to achieves <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-112-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1393" role="math" style="width: 3.426em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.066em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1003.01em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1394"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1395"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1396"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1397" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&lt;</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1398" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.243em;">−</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1399" style="padding-left: 0.243em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1400"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1401"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1402"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1403" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">80</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.13em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-112">{&lt;} -{\hbox{80}}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>-dBc spur suppression with 25-dBm transmit power at 920 MHz in the TX, which complies with the most stringent regulatory spectral mask without a SAW filter.</p></div>
<h3>ACKNOWLEDGEMENT</h3><p>The authors would like to thank J. Jung and J. Yi, both with PHYCHIPS Inc., Daejeon, Korea, for the chip layout and interference analysis of the cellular networks, respectively.</p></div></div>

<script>

function getCookie(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
}

j$('document').ready(function(){
	if(getCookie('legacyUserName')!=null)
	{
		if(IBP_WS_ENABLED_FLAG){
		Modal.refreshLegacyAccountTransition('/xpl/mwLegacyAccountTransition.jsp');
		}
	}
});

</script>
